<own>
<not id="K9Bu9oO6f066Law7X/bEJg" >
<dsc reserve="142" >The packages above are dependent on one or more &quot;common&quot; packages that contain types and/or methods used by more than one architectural layer.</dsc>
</not>
<not id="G6HJi26xLkaSlqovXdchFw" >
<dsc reserve="153" >InstrumentControl represents the &quot;control layer&quot; for the instrument.  It provides for connection to the actual control layer (non-.NET code) via XML-RPC.</dsc>
</not>
<not id="RCJDAo9fCkeCKCEjsISb/w" >
<dsc reserve="192" >Separator represents the &quot;business layer&quot; for the instrument.  It provides a high-level view of the instrument.  Graphical (and in future, non-graphical) clients connect via the Separator API.</dsc>
</not>
<not id="lV0cqkSYF0iEQHFqwFJgOg" >
<dsc>OperatorConsole is the on-board GUI.</dsc>
</not>
</own>
